NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
OCKHAM INDIA CLINICAL RESEARCH AND DATA SERVICES PRIVATE LIMITED
REGD. OFF.: 4TH FLOOR, PRAKASH PRESIDIUM, 110 MAHATMA GANDHI ROAD, NUNGAMBAKKAM,
CHENNAI-600 034.
In the matter of Section 485 of Companies Act, 1956 and Rule 315 of The Companies (Court) Rules, 1959
NOTICE OF APPOINTMENT OF LIQUIDATOR
Notice is hereby given to the General Public that the shareholders of the Company at the extraordinary general
meeting held on 30th day of December, 2016 at 11.00 AM has passed the following resolution for voluntary winding up of
the Company under sections 484 and 490 under the Companies Act, 1956 and has also appointed Mr. Harishankar Mani,
Advocate as the liquidator of the company, who has forthwith taken over the affairs of the company and initiate proceeding
to wind up the company.
Resolution passed by the Shareholders:
“Resolved That pursuant to the provisions of Section 484(1)(b) and other applicable provisions, if any, of the
Companies Act, 1956 (including any statutory modifications thereto or re-enactment thereof), consent of the Company be
and is hereby accorded to Wind up the Company Voluntarily with effect from 30-12-2016.”

Jan. 18, 2017]
